</span><span id="L-102"><a href="#L-102"><span class="linenos">102</span></a>
</span><span id="L-103"><a href="#L-103"><span class="linenos">103</span></a>            <span class="c1"># Newer versions of Memphis take a user of the form</span>
</span><span id="L-104"><a href="#L-104"><span class="linenos">104</span></a>            <span class="c1"># &quot;{username}${account_id}&quot;.  For older versions, the user was</span>
</span><span id="L-105"><a href="#L-105"><span class="linenos">105</span></a>            <span class="c1"># simply the username.  The user is created using the new style</span>
</span><span id="L-106"><a href="#L-106"><span class="linenos">106</span></a>            <span class="c1"># in Memphis.connect(). If connecting with the new-style user</span>
</span><span id="L-107"><a href="#L-107"><span class="linenos">107</span></a>            <span class="c1"># fails, try the old style.</span>

</span><span id="L-143"><a href="#L-143"><span class="linenos">143</span></a>        <span class="n">key_file</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">str</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="s2">&quot;&quot;</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="L-144"><a href="#L-144"><span class="linenos">144</span></a>        <span class="n">ca_file</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">str</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="s2">&quot;&quot;</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="L-145"><a href="#L-145"><span class="linenos">145</span></a>    <span class="p">):</span>
</span><span id="L-146"><a href="#L-146"><span class="linenos">146</span></a><span class="w">        </span><span class="sd">&quot;&quot;&quot;Creates connection with Memphis.</span>
</span><span id="L-147"><a href="#L-147"><span class="linenos">147</span></a><span class="sd">        Args:</span>
</span><span id="L-148"><a href="#L-148"><span class="linenos">148</span></a><span class="sd">            host (str): memphis host.</span>
</span><span id="L-149"><a href="#L-149"><span class="linenos">149</span></a><span class="sd">            username (str): user of type root/application.</span>
</span><span id="L-150"><a href="#L-150"><span class="linenos">150</span></a><span class="sd">            account_id (int): You can find it on the profile page in the Memphis UI. This field should be sent only on the cloud version of Memphis, otherwise it will be ignored</span>
</span><span id="L-151"><a href="#L-151"><span class="linenos">151</span></a><span class="sd">            connection_token (str): connection token.</span>
</span><span id="L-152"><a href="#L-152"><span class="linenos">152</span></a><span class="sd">            password (str): depends on how Memphis deployed - default is connection token-based authentication.</span>
</span><span id="L-153"><a href="#L-153"><span class="linenos">153</span></a><span class="sd">            port (int, optional): port. Defaults to 6666.</span>
</span><span id="L-154"><a href="#L-154"><span class="linenos">154</span></a><span class="sd">            reconnect (bool, optional): whether to do reconnect while connection is lost. Defaults to True.</span>
</span><span id="L-155"><a href="#L-155"><span class="linenos">155</span></a><span class="sd">            max_reconnect (int, optional): The reconnect attempt. Defaults to 3.</span>
</span><span id="L-156"><a href="#L-156"><span class="linenos">156</span></a><span class="sd">            reconnect_interval_ms (int, optional): Interval in milliseconds between reconnect attempts. Defaults to 200.</span>
</span><span id="L-157"><a href="#L-157"><span class="linenos">157</span></a><span class="sd">            timeout_ms (int, optional): connection timeout in milliseconds. Defaults to 15000.</span>
</span><span id="L-158"><a href="#L-158"><span class="linenos">158</span></a><span class="sd">            key_file (string): path to tls key file.</span>
</span><span id="L-159"><a href="#L-159"><span class="linenos">159</span></a><span class="sd">            cert_file (string): path to tls cert file.</span>
</span><span id="L-160"><a href="#L-160"><span class="linenos">160</span></a><span class="sd">            ca_file (string): path to tls ca file.</span>
</span><span id="L-161"><a href="#L-161"><span class="linenos">161</span></a><span class="sd">        &quot;&quot;&quot;</span>
</span><span id="L-162"><a href="#L-162"><span class="linenos">162</span></a>        <span class="bp">self</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">host</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="bp">self</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">__normalize_host</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">host</span><span class="p">)</span>

</span><span id="L-532"><a href="#L-532"><span class="linenos">532</span></a>    <span class="k">async</span> <span class="k">def</span> <span class="nf">consumer</span><span class="p">(</span>
</span><span id="L-533"><a href="#L-533"><span class="linenos">533</span></a>        <span class="bp">self</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="L-534"><a href="#L-534"><span class="linenos">534</span></a>        <span class="n">station_name</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">str</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="L-535"><a href="#L-535"><span class="linenos">535</span></a>        <span class="n">consumer_name</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">str</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="L-536"><a href="#L-536"><span class="linenos">536</span></a>        <span class="n">consumer_group</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">str</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="s2">&quot;&quot;</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="L-537"><a href="#L-537"><span class="linenos">537</span></a>        <span class="n">pull_interval_ms</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">int</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">1000</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="L-538"><a href="#L-538"><span class="linenos">538</span></a>        <span class="n">batch_size</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">int</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">10</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="L-539"><a href="#L-539"><span class="linenos">539</span></a>        <span class="n">batch_max_time_to_wait_ms</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">int</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">5000</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="L-540"><a href="#L-540"><span class="linenos">540</span></a>        <span class="n">max_ack_time_ms</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">int</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">30000</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="L-541"><a href="#L-541"><span class="linenos">541</span></a>        <span class="n">max_msg_deliveries</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">int</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">10</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="L-542"><a href="#L-542"><span class="linenos">542</span></a>        <span class="n">generate_random_suffix</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">bool</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="kc">False</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="L-543"><a href="#L-543"><span class="linenos">543</span></a>        <span class="n">start_consume_from_sequence</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">int</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="L-544"><a href="#L-544"><span class="linenos">544</span></a>        <span class="n">last_messages</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">int</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="L-545"><a href="#L-545"><span class="linenos">545</span></a>    <span class="p">):</span>
</span><span id="L-546"><a href="#L-546"><span class="linenos">546</span></a><span class="w">        </span><span class="sd">&quot;&quot;&quot;Creates a consumer.</span>
</span><span id="L-547"><a href="#L-547"><span class="linenos">547</span></a><span class="sd">        Args:.</span>
</span><span id="L-548"><a href="#L-548"><span class="linenos">548</span></a><span class="sd">            station_name (str): station name to consume messages from.</span>
</span><span id="L-549"><a href="#L-549"><span class="linenos">549</span></a><span class="sd">            consumer_name (str): name for the consumer.</span>
</span><span id="L-550"><a href="#L-550"><span class="linenos">550</span></a><span class="sd">            consumer_group (str, optional): consumer group name. Defaults to the consumer name.</span>
</span><span id="L-551"><a href="#L-551"><span class="linenos">551</span></a><span class="sd">            pull_interval_ms (int, optional): interval in milliseconds between pulls. Defaults to 1000.</span>
</span><span id="L-552"><a href="#L-552"><span class="linenos">552</span></a><span class="sd">            batch_size (int, optional): pull batch size. Defaults to 10.</span>
</span><span id="L-553"><a href="#L-553"><span class="linenos">553</span></a><span class="sd">            batch_max_time_to_wait_ms (int, optional): max time in milliseconds to wait between pulls. Defaults to 5000.</span>
</span><span id="L-554"><a href="#L-554"><span class="linenos">554</span></a><span class="sd">            max_ack_time_ms (int, optional): max time for ack a message in milliseconds, in case a message not acked in this time period the Memphis broker will resend it. Defaults to 30000.</span>
</span><span id="L-555"><a href="#L-555"><span class="linenos">555</span></a><span class="sd">            max_msg_deliveries (int, optional): max number of message deliveries, by default is 10.</span>
</span><span id="L-556"><a href="#L-556"><span class="linenos">556</span></a><span class="sd">            generate_random_suffix (bool): false by default, if true concatenate a random suffix to consumer&#39;s name</span>
</span><span id="L-557"><a href="#L-557"><span class="linenos">557</span></a><span class="sd">            start_consume_from_sequence(int, optional): start consuming from a specific sequence. defaults to 1.</span>
</span><span id="L-558"><a href="#L-558"><span class="linenos">558</span></a><span class="sd">            last_messages: consume the last N messages, defaults to -1 (all messages in the station).</span>
</span><span id="L-559"><a href="#L-559"><span class="linenos">559</span></a><span class="sd">        Returns:</span>
</span><span id="L-560"><a href="#L-560"><span class="linenos">560</span></a><span class="sd">            object: consumer</span>
</span><span id="L-561"><a href="#L-561"><span class="linenos">561</span></a><span class="sd">        &quot;&quot;&quot;</span>
</span><span id="L-562"><a href="#L-562"><span class="linenos">562</span></a>        <span class="k">try</span><span class="p">:</span>
</span><span id="L-563"><a href="#L-563"><span class="linenos">563</span></a>            <span class="k">if</span> <span class="ow">not</span> <span class="bp">self</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">is_connection_active</span><span class="p">:</span>
</span><span id="L-564"><a href="#L-564"><span class="linenos">564</span></a>                <span class="k">raise</span> <span class="n">MemphisError</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s2">&quot;Connection is dead&quot;</span><span class="p">)</span>
</span><span id="L-565"><a href="#L-565"><span class="linenos">565</span></a>            <span class="k">if</span> <span class="n">batch_size</span> <span class="o">&gt;</span> <span class="bp">self</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">MAX_BATCH_SIZE</span><span class="p">:</span>
</span><span id="L-566"><a href="#L-566"><span class="linenos">566</span></a>                <span class="k">raise</span> <span class="n">MemphisError</span><span class="p">(</span>
</span><span id="L-567"><a href="#L-567"><span class="linenos">567</span></a>                    <span class="sa">f</span><span class="s2">&quot;Batch size can not be greater than </span><span class="si">{</span><span class="bp">self</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">MAX_BATCH_SIZE</span><span class="si">}</span><span class="s2">&quot;</span><span class="p">)</span>
</span><span id="L-568"><a href="#L-568"><span class="linenos">568</span></a>            <span class="n">real_name</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">consumer_name</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">lower</span><span class="p">()</span>
</span><span id="L-569"><a href="#L-569"><span class="linenos">569</span></a>            <span class="k">if</span> <span class="n">generate_random_suffix</span><span class="p">:</span>
</span><span id="L-570"><a href="#L-570"><span class="linenos">570</span></a>                <span class="n">consumer_name</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="bp">self</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">__generate_random_suffix</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">consumer_name</span><span class="p">)</span>
</span><span id="L-571"><a href="#L-571"><span class="linenos">571</span></a>            <span class="n">cg</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">consumer_name</span> <span class="k">if</span> <span class="ow">not</span> <span class="n">consumer_group</span> <span class="k">else</span> <span class="n">consumer_group</span>
</span><span id="L-572"><a href="#L-572"><span class="linenos">572</span></a>
</span><span id="L-573"><a href="#L-573"><span class="linenos">573</span></a>            <span class="k">if</span> <span class="n">start_consume_from_sequence</span> <span class="o">&lt;=</span> <span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">:</span>
</span><span id="L-574"><a href="#L-574"><span class="linenos">574</span></a>                <span class="k">raise</span> <span class="n">MemphisError</span><span class="p">(</span>
</span><span id="L-575"><a href="#L-575"><span class="linenos">575</span></a>                    <span class="s2">&quot;start_consume_from_sequence has to be a positive number&quot;</span>
</span><span id="L-576"><a href="#L-576"><span class="linenos">576</span></a>                <span class="p">)</span>
</span><span id="L-577"><a href="#L-577"><span class="linenos">577</span></a>
</span><span id="L-578"><a href="#L-578"><span class="linenos">578</span></a>            <span class="k">if</span> <span class="n">last_messages</span> <span class="o">&lt;</span> <span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">:</span>
</span><span id="L-579"><a href="#L-579"><span class="linenos">579</span></a>                <span class="k">raise</span> <span class="n">MemphisError</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s2">&quot;min value for last_messages is -1&quot;</span><span class="p">)</span>
</span><span id="L-580"><a href="#L-580"><span class="linenos">580</span></a>
</span><span id="L-581"><a href="#L-581"><span class="linenos">581</span></a>            <span class="k">if</span> <span class="n">start_consume_from_sequence</span> <span class="o">&gt;</span> <span class="mi">1</span> <span class="ow">and</span> <span class="n">last_messages</span> <span class="o">&gt;</span> <span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">:</span>
</span><span id="L-582"><a href="#L-582"><span class="linenos">582</span></a>                <span class="k">raise</span> <span class="n">MemphisError</span><span class="p">(</span>
</span><span id="L-583"><a href="#L-583"><span class="linenos">583</span></a>                    <span class="s2">&quot;Consumer creation options can&#39;t contain both start_consume_from_sequence and last_messages&quot;</span>
</span><span id="L-584"><a href="#L-584"><span class="linenos">584</span></a>                <span class="p">)</span>
</span><span id="L-585"><a href="#L-585"><span class="linenos">585</span></a>            <span class="n">create_consumer_req</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="p">{</span>
</span><span id="L-586"><a href="#L-586"><span class="linenos">586</span></a>                <span class="s2">&quot;name&quot;</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">consumer_name</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="L-587"><a href="#L-587"><span class="linenos">587</span></a>                <span class="s2">&quot;station_name&quot;</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">station_name</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="L-588"><a href="#L-588"><span class="linenos">588</span></a>                <span class="s2">&quot;connection_id&quot;</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="bp">self</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">connection_id</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="L-589"><a href="#L-589"><span class="linenos">589</span></a>                <span class="s2">&quot;consumer_type&quot;</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="s2">&quot;application&quot;</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="L-590"><a href="#L-590"><span class="linenos">590</span></a>                <span class="s2">&quot;consumers_group&quot;</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">consumer_group</span><span class="p">,</span>

</span><span id="L-630"><a href="#L-630"><span class="linenos">630</span></a>    <span class="k">async</span> <span class="k">def</span> <span class="nf">produce</span><span class="p">(</span>
</span><span id="L-631"><a href="#L-631"><span class="linenos">631</span></a>        <span class="bp">self</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="L-632"><a href="#L-632"><span class="linenos">632</span></a>        <span class="n">station_name</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">str</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="L-633"><a href="#L-633"><span class="linenos">633</span></a>        <span class="n">producer_name</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">str</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="L-634"><a href="#L-634"><span class="linenos">634</span></a>        <span class="n">message</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="L-635"><a href="#L-635"><span class="linenos">635</span></a>        <span class="n">generate_random_suffix</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">bool</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="kc">False</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="L-636"><a href="#L-636"><span class="linenos">636</span></a>        <span class="n">ack_wait_sec</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">int</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">15</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="L-637"><a href="#L-637"><span class="linenos">637</span></a>        <span class="n">headers</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">Union</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">Headers</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="kc">None</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="kc">None</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="L-638"><a href="#L-638"><span class="linenos">638</span></a>        <span class="n">async_produce</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">bool</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="kc">False</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="L-639"><a href="#L-639"><span class="linenos">639</span></a>        <span class="n">msg_id</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">Union</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="nb">str</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="kc">None</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="kc">None</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="L-640"><a href="#L-640"><span class="linenos">640</span></a>    <span class="p">):</span>
</span><span id="L-641"><a href="#L-641"><span class="linenos">641</span></a><span class="w">        </span><span class="sd">&quot;&quot;&quot;Produces a message into a station without the need to create a producer.</span>
</span><span id="L-642"><a href="#L-642"><span class="linenos">642</span></a><span class="sd">        Args:</span>
</span><span id="L-643"><a href="#L-643"><span class="linenos">643</span></a><span class="sd">            station_name (str): station name to produce messages into.</span>
</span><span id="L-644"><a href="#L-644"><span class="linenos">644</span></a><span class="sd">            producer_name (str): name for the producer.</span>
</span><span id="L-645"><a href="#L-645"><span class="linenos">645</span></a><span class="sd">            message (bytearray/dict): message to send into the station - bytearray/protobuf class (schema validated station - protobuf) or bytearray/dict (schema validated station - json schema) or string/bytearray/graphql.language.ast.DocumentNode (schema validated station - graphql schema or  bytearray/dict (schema validated station - avro schema))</span>
</span><span id="L-646"><a href="#L-646"><span class="linenos">646</span></a><span class="sd">            generate_random_suffix (bool): false by default, if true concatenate a random suffix to producer&#39;s name</span>
</span><span id="L-647"><a href="#L-647"><span class="linenos">647</span></a><span class="sd">            ack_wait_sec (int, optional): max time in seconds to wait for an ack from memphis. Defaults to 15.</span>
</span><span id="L-648"><a href="#L-648"><span class="linenos">648</span></a><span class="sd">            headers (dict, optional): Message headers, defaults to {}.</span>
</span><span id="L-649"><a href="#L-649"><span class="linenos">649</span></a><span class="sd">            async_produce (boolean, optional): produce operation won&#39;t wait for broker acknowledgement</span>
</span><span id="L-650"><a href="#L-650"><span class="linenos">650</span></a><span class="sd">            msg_id (string, optional): Attach msg-id header to the message in order to achieve idempotence</span>
</span><span id="L-651"><a href="#L-651"><span class="linenos">651</span></a><span class="sd">        Raises:</span>
</span><span id="L-652"><a href="#L-652"><span class="linenos">652</span></a><span class="sd">            Exception: _description_</span>
</span><span id="L-653"><a href="#L-653"><span class="linenos">653</span></a><span class="sd">        &quot;&quot;&quot;</span>
</span><span id="L-654"><a href="#L-654"><span class="linenos">654</span></a>        <span class="k">try</span><span class="p">:</span>
</span><span id="L-655"><a href="#L-655"><span class="linenos">655</span></a>            <span class="n">internal_station_name</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">get_internal_name</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">station_name</span><span class="p">)</span>
</span><span id="L-656"><a href="#L-656"><span class="linenos">656</span></a>            <span class="n">map_key</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">internal_station_name</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="s2">&quot;_&quot;</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="n">producer_name</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">lower</span><span class="p">()</span>
</span><span id="L-657"><a href="#L-657"><span class="linenos">657</span></a>            <span class="n">producer</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="kc">None</span>
</span><span id="L-658"><a href="#L-658"><span class="linenos">658</span></a>            <span class="k">if</span> <span class="n">map_key</span> <span class="ow">in</span> <span class="bp">self</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">producers_map</span><span class="p">:</span>
</span><span id="L-659"><a href="#L-659"><span class="linenos">659</span></a>                <span class="n">producer</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="bp">self</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">producers_map</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">map_key</span><span class="p">]</span>
</span><span id="L-660"><a href="#L-660"><span class="linenos">660</span></a>            <span class="k">else</span><span class="p">:</span>
</span><span id="L-661"><a href="#L-661"><span class="linenos">661</span></a>                <span class="n">producer</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="k">await</span> <span class="bp">self</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">producer</span><span class="p">(</span>
</span><span id="L-662"><a href="#L-662"><span class="linenos">662</span></a>                    <span class="n">station_name</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="n">station_name</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="L-663"><a href="#L-663"><span class="linenos">663</span></a>                    <span class="n">producer_name</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="n">producer_name</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="L-664"><a href="#L-664"><span class="linenos">664</span></a>                    <span class="n">generate_random_suffix</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="n">generate_random_suffix</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="L-665"><a href="#L-665"><span class="linenos">665</span></a>                <span class="p">)</span>
</span><span id="L-666"><a href="#L-666"><span class="linenos">666</span></a>            <span class="k">await</span> <span class="n">producer</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">produce</span><span class="p">(</span>
</span><span id="L-667"><a href="#L-667"><span class="linenos">667</span></a>                <span class="n">message</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="n">message</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="L-668"><a href="#L-668"><span class="linenos">668</span></a>                <span class="n">ack_wait_sec</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="n">ack_wait_sec</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="L-669"><a href="#L-669"><span class="linenos">669</span></a>                <span class="n">headers</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="n">headers</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="L-670"><a href="#L-670"><span class="linenos">670</span></a>                <span class="n">async_produce</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="n">async_produce</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="L-671"><a href="#L-671"><span class="linenos">671</span></a>                <span class="n">msg_id</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="n">msg_id</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="L-672"><a href="#L-672"><span class="linenos">672</span></a>            <span class="p">)</span>
</span><span id="L-673"><a href="#L-673"><span class="linenos">673</span></a>        <span class="k">except</span> <span class="ne">Exception</span> <span class="k">as</span> <span class="n">e</span><span class="p">:</span>
</span><span id="L-674"><a href="#L-674"><span class="linenos">674</span></a>            <span class="k">raise</span> <span class="n">MemphisError</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="nb">str</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">e</span><span class="p">))</span> <span class="kn">from</span> <span class="nn">e</span>
</span><span id="L-675"><a href="#L-675"><span class="linenos">675</span></a>
</span><span id="L-676"><a href="#L-676"><span class="linenos">676</span></a>    <span class="k">async</span> <span class="k">def</span> <span class="nf">fetch_messages</span><span class="p">(</span>
</span><span id="L-677"><a href="#L-677"><span class="linenos">677</span></a>        <span class="bp">self</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="L-678"><a href="#L-678"><span class="linenos">678</span></a>        <span class="n">station_name</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">str</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="L-679"><a href="#L-679"><span class="linenos">679</span></a>        <span class="n">consumer_name</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">str</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="L-680"><a href="#L-680"><span class="linenos">680</span></a>        <span class="n">consumer_group</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">str</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="s2">&quot;&quot;</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="L-681"><a href="#L-681"><span class="linenos">681</span></a>        <span class="n">batch_size</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">int</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">10</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="L-682"><a href="#L-682"><span class="linenos">682</span></a>        <span class="n">batch_max_time_to_wait_ms</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">int</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">5000</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="L-683"><a href="#L-683"><span class="linenos">683</span></a>        <span class="n">max_ack_time_ms</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">int</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">30000</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="L-684"><a href="#L-684"><span class="linenos">684</span></a>        <span class="n">max_msg_deliveries</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">int</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">10</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="L-685"><a href="#L-685"><span class="linenos">685</span></a>        <span class="n">generate_random_suffix</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">bool</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="kc">False</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="L-686"><a href="#L-686"><span class="linenos">686</span></a>        <span class="n">start_consume_from_sequence</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">int</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="L-687"><a href="#L-687"><span class="linenos">687</span></a>        <span class="n">last_messages</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">int</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="L-688"><a href="#L-688"><span class="linenos">688</span></a>    <span class="p">):</span>
</span><span id="L-689"><a href="#L-689"><span class="linenos">689</span></a><span class="w">        </span><span class="sd">&quot;&quot;&quot;Consume a batch of messages.</span>
</span><span id="L-690"><a href="#L-690"><span class="linenos">690</span></a><span class="sd">        Args:.</span>
</span><span id="L-691"><a href="#L-691"><span class="linenos">691</span></a><span class="sd">            station_name (str): station name to consume messages from.</span>
</span><span id="L-692"><a href="#L-692"><span class="linenos">692</span></a><span class="sd">            consumer_name (str): name for the consumer.</span>
</span><span id="L-693"><a href="#L-693"><span class="linenos">693</span></a><span class="sd">            consumer_group (str, optional): consumer group name. Defaults to the consumer name.</span>
</span><span id="L-694"><a href="#L-694"><span class="linenos">694</span></a><span class="sd">            batch_size (int, optional): pull batch size. Defaults to 10.</span>
</span><span id="L-695"><a href="#L-695"><span class="linenos">695</span></a><span class="sd">            batch_max_time_to_wait_ms (int, optional): max time in miliseconds to wait between pulls. Defaults to 5000.</span>
</span><span id="L-696"><a href="#L-696"><span class="linenos">696</span></a><span class="sd">            max_ack_time_ms (int, optional): max time for ack a message in miliseconds, in case a message not acked in this time period the Memphis broker will resend it. Defaults to 30000.</span>
</span><span id="L-697"><a href="#L-697"><span class="linenos">697</span></a><span class="sd">            max_msg_deliveries (int, optional): max number of message deliveries, by default is 10.</span>
</span><span id="L-698"><a href="#L-698"><span class="linenos">698</span></a><span class="sd">            generate_random_suffix (bool): false by default, if true concatenate a random suffix to consumer&#39;s name</span>
</span><span id="L-699"><a href="#L-699"><span class="linenos">699</span></a><span class="sd">            start_consume_from_sequence(int, optional): start consuming from a specific sequence. defaults to 1.</span>
</span><span id="L-700"><a href="#L-700"><span class="linenos">700</span></a><span class="sd">            last_messages: consume the last N messages, defaults to -1 (all messages in the station).</span>
</span><span id="L-701"><a href="#L-701"><span class="linenos">701</span></a><span class="sd">        Returns:</span>
</span><span id="L-702"><a href="#L-702"><span class="linenos">702</span></a><span class="sd">            list: Message</span>
</span><span id="L-703"><a href="#L-703"><span class="linenos">703</span></a><span class="sd">        &quot;&quot;&quot;</span>
</span><span id="L-704"><a href="#L-704"><span class="linenos">704</span></a>        <span class="k">try</span><span class="p">:</span>

</span><span id="Memphis-140"><a href="#Memphis-140"><span class="linenos">140</span></a>        <span class="n">max_reconnect</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">int</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">10</span><span class="p">,</span>

</span><span id="Memphis-144"><a href="#Memphis-144"><span class="linenos">144</span></a>        <span class="n">key_file</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">str</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="s2">&quot;&quot;</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-145"><a href="#Memphis-145"><span class="linenos">145</span></a>        <span class="n">ca_file</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">str</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="s2">&quot;&quot;</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-146"><a href="#Memphis-146"><span class="linenos">146</span></a>    <span class="p">):</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-147"><a href="#Memphis-147"><span class="linenos">147</span></a><span class="w">        </span><span class="sd">&quot;&quot;&quot;Creates connection with Memphis.</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-148"><a href="#Memphis-148"><span class="linenos">148</span></a><span class="sd">        Args:</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-149"><a href="#Memphis-149"><span class="linenos">149</span></a><span class="sd">            host (str): memphis host.</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-150"><a href="#Memphis-150"><span class="linenos">150</span></a><span class="sd">            username (str): user of type root/application.</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-151"><a href="#Memphis-151"><span class="linenos">151</span></a><span class="sd">            account_id (int): You can find it on the profile page in the Memphis UI. This field should be sent only on the cloud version of Memphis, otherwise it will be ignored</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-152"><a href="#Memphis-152"><span class="linenos">152</span></a><span class="sd">            connection_token (str): connection token.</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-153"><a href="#Memphis-153"><span class="linenos">153</span></a><span class="sd">            password (str): depends on how Memphis deployed - default is connection token-based authentication.</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-154"><a href="#Memphis-154"><span class="linenos">154</span></a><span class="sd">            port (int, optional): port. Defaults to 6666.</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-155"><a href="#Memphis-155"><span class="linenos">155</span></a><span class="sd">            reconnect (bool, optional): whether to do reconnect while connection is lost. Defaults to True.</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-156"><a href="#Memphis-156"><span class="linenos">156</span></a><span class="sd">            max_reconnect (int, optional): The reconnect attempt. Defaults to 3.</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-157"><a href="#Memphis-157"><span class="linenos">157</span></a><span class="sd">            reconnect_interval_ms (int, optional): Interval in milliseconds between reconnect attempts. Defaults to 200.</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-158"><a href="#Memphis-158"><span class="linenos">158</span></a><span class="sd">            timeout_ms (int, optional): connection timeout in milliseconds. Defaults to 15000.</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-159"><a href="#Memphis-159"><span class="linenos">159</span></a><span class="sd">            key_file (string): path to tls key file.</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-160"><a href="#Memphis-160"><span class="linenos">160</span></a><span class="sd">            cert_file (string): path to tls cert file.</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-161"><a href="#Memphis-161"><span class="linenos">161</span></a><span class="sd">            ca_file (string): path to tls ca file.</span>

</span><span id="Memphis-533"><a href="#Memphis-533"><span class="linenos">533</span></a>    <span class="k">async</span> <span class="k">def</span> <span class="nf">consumer</span><span class="p">(</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-534"><a href="#Memphis-534"><span class="linenos">534</span></a>        <span class="bp">self</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-535"><a href="#Memphis-535"><span class="linenos">535</span></a>        <span class="n">station_name</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">str</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-536"><a href="#Memphis-536"><span class="linenos">536</span></a>        <span class="n">consumer_name</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">str</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-537"><a href="#Memphis-537"><span class="linenos">537</span></a>        <span class="n">consumer_group</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">str</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="s2">&quot;&quot;</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-538"><a href="#Memphis-538"><span class="linenos">538</span></a>        <span class="n">pull_interval_ms</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">int</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">1000</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-539"><a href="#Memphis-539"><span class="linenos">539</span></a>        <span class="n">batch_size</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">int</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">10</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-540"><a href="#Memphis-540"><span class="linenos">540</span></a>        <span class="n">batch_max_time_to_wait_ms</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">int</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">5000</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-541"><a href="#Memphis-541"><span class="linenos">541</span></a>        <span class="n">max_ack_time_ms</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">int</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">30000</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-542"><a href="#Memphis-542"><span class="linenos">542</span></a>        <span class="n">max_msg_deliveries</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">int</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">10</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-543"><a href="#Memphis-543"><span class="linenos">543</span></a>        <span class="n">generate_random_suffix</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">bool</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="kc">False</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-544"><a href="#Memphis-544"><span class="linenos">544</span></a>        <span class="n">start_consume_from_sequence</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">int</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-545"><a href="#Memphis-545"><span class="linenos">545</span></a>        <span class="n">last_messages</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">int</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-546"><a href="#Memphis-546"><span class="linenos">546</span></a>    <span class="p">):</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-547"><a href="#Memphis-547"><span class="linenos">547</span></a><span class="w">        </span><span class="sd">&quot;&quot;&quot;Creates a consumer.</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-548"><a href="#Memphis-548"><span class="linenos">548</span></a><span class="sd">        Args:.</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-549"><a href="#Memphis-549"><span class="linenos">549</span></a><span class="sd">            station_name (str): station name to consume messages from.</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-550"><a href="#Memphis-550"><span class="linenos">550</span></a><span class="sd">            consumer_name (str): name for the consumer.</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-551"><a href="#Memphis-551"><span class="linenos">551</span></a><span class="sd">            consumer_group (str, optional): consumer group name. Defaults to the consumer name.</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-552"><a href="#Memphis-552"><span class="linenos">552</span></a><span class="sd">            pull_interval_ms (int, optional): interval in milliseconds between pulls. Defaults to 1000.</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-553"><a href="#Memphis-553"><span class="linenos">553</span></a><span class="sd">            batch_size (int, optional): pull batch size. Defaults to 10.</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-554"><a href="#Memphis-554"><span class="linenos">554</span></a><span class="sd">            batch_max_time_to_wait_ms (int, optional): max time in milliseconds to wait between pulls. Defaults to 5000.</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-555"><a href="#Memphis-555"><span class="linenos">555</span></a><span class="sd">            max_ack_time_ms (int, optional): max time for ack a message in milliseconds, in case a message not acked in this time period the Memphis broker will resend it. Defaults to 30000.</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-556"><a href="#Memphis-556"><span class="linenos">556</span></a><span class="sd">            max_msg_deliveries (int, optional): max number of message deliveries, by default is 10.</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-557"><a href="#Memphis-557"><span class="linenos">557</span></a><span class="sd">            generate_random_suffix (bool): false by default, if true concatenate a random suffix to consumer&#39;s name</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-558"><a href="#Memphis-558"><span class="linenos">558</span></a><span class="sd">            start_consume_from_sequence(int, optional): start consuming from a specific sequence. defaults to 1.</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-559"><a href="#Memphis-559"><span class="linenos">559</span></a><span class="sd">            last_messages: consume the last N messages, defaults to -1 (all messages in the station).</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-560"><a href="#Memphis-560"><span class="linenos">560</span></a><span class="sd">        Returns:</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-561"><a href="#Memphis-561"><span class="linenos">561</span></a><span class="sd">            object: consumer</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-562"><a href="#Memphis-562"><span class="linenos">562</span></a><span class="sd">        &quot;&quot;&quot;</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-563"><a href="#Memphis-563"><span class="linenos">563</span></a>        <span class="k">try</span><span class="p">:</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-564"><a href="#Memphis-564"><span class="linenos">564</span></a>            <span class="k">if</span> <span class="ow">not</span> <span class="bp">self</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">is_connection_active</span><span class="p">:</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-565"><a href="#Memphis-565"><span class="linenos">565</span></a>                <span class="k">raise</span> <span class="n">MemphisError</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s2">&quot;Connection is dead&quot;</span><span class="p">)</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-566"><a href="#Memphis-566"><span class="linenos">566</span></a>            <span class="k">if</span> <span class="n">batch_size</span> <span class="o">&gt;</span> <span class="bp">self</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">MAX_BATCH_SIZE</span><span class="p">:</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-567"><a href="#Memphis-567"><span class="linenos">567</span></a>                <span class="k">raise</span> <span class="n">MemphisError</span><span class="p">(</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-568"><a href="#Memphis-568"><span class="linenos">568</span></a>                    <span class="sa">f</span><span class="s2">&quot;Batch size can not be greater than </span><span class="si">{</span><span class="bp">self</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">MAX_BATCH_SIZE</span><span class="si">}</span><span class="s2">&quot;</span><span class="p">)</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-569"><a href="#Memphis-569"><span class="linenos">569</span></a>            <span class="n">real_name</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">consumer_name</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">lower</span><span class="p">()</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-570"><a href="#Memphis-570"><span class="linenos">570</span></a>            <span class="k">if</span> <span class="n">generate_random_suffix</span><span class="p">:</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-571"><a href="#Memphis-571"><span class="linenos">571</span></a>                <span class="n">consumer_name</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="bp">self</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">__generate_random_suffix</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">consumer_name</span><span class="p">)</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-572"><a href="#Memphis-572"><span class="linenos">572</span></a>            <span class="n">cg</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">consumer_name</span> <span class="k">if</span> <span class="ow">not</span> <span class="n">consumer_group</span> <span class="k">else</span> <span class="n">consumer_group</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-573"><a href="#Memphis-573"><span class="linenos">573</span></a>
</span><span id="Memphis-574"><a href="#Memphis-574"><span class="linenos">574</span></a>            <span class="k">if</span> <span class="n">start_consume_from_sequence</span> <span class="o">&lt;=</span> <span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">:</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-575"><a href="#Memphis-575"><span class="linenos">575</span></a>                <span class="k">raise</span> <span class="n">MemphisError</span><span class="p">(</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-576"><a href="#Memphis-576"><span class="linenos">576</span></a>                    <span class="s2">&quot;start_consume_from_sequence has to be a positive number&quot;</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-577"><a href="#Memphis-577"><span class="linenos">577</span></a>                <span class="p">)</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-578"><a href="#Memphis-578"><span class="linenos">578</span></a>
</span><span id="Memphis-579"><a href="#Memphis-579"><span class="linenos">579</span></a>            <span class="k">if</span> <span class="n">last_messages</span> <span class="o">&lt;</span> <span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">:</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-580"><a href="#Memphis-580"><span class="linenos">580</span></a>                <span class="k">raise</span> <span class="n">MemphisError</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s2">&quot;min value for last_messages is -1&quot;</span><span class="p">)</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-581"><a href="#Memphis-581"><span class="linenos">581</span></a>
</span><span id="Memphis-582"><a href="#Memphis-582"><span class="linenos">582</span></a>            <span class="k">if</span> <span class="n">start_consume_from_sequence</span> <span class="o">&gt;</span> <span class="mi">1</span> <span class="ow">and</span> <span class="n">last_messages</span> <span class="o">&gt;</span> <span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">:</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-583"><a href="#Memphis-583"><span class="linenos">583</span></a>                <span class="k">raise</span> <span class="n">MemphisError</span><span class="p">(</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-584"><a href="#Memphis-584"><span class="linenos">584</span></a>                    <span class="s2">&quot;Consumer creation options can&#39;t contain both start_consume_from_sequence and last_messages&quot;</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-585"><a href="#Memphis-585"><span class="linenos">585</span></a>                <span class="p">)</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-586"><a href="#Memphis-586"><span class="linenos">586</span></a>            <span class="n">create_consumer_req</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="p">{</span>

</span><span id="Memphis-631"><a href="#Memphis-631"><span class="linenos">631</span></a>    <span class="k">async</span> <span class="k">def</span> <span class="nf">produce</span><span class="p">(</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-632"><a href="#Memphis-632"><span class="linenos">632</span></a>        <span class="bp">self</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-633"><a href="#Memphis-633"><span class="linenos">633</span></a>        <span class="n">station_name</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">str</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-634"><a href="#Memphis-634"><span class="linenos">634</span></a>        <span class="n">producer_name</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">str</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-635"><a href="#Memphis-635"><span class="linenos">635</span></a>        <span class="n">message</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-636"><a href="#Memphis-636"><span class="linenos">636</span></a>        <span class="n">generate_random_suffix</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">bool</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="kc">False</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-637"><a href="#Memphis-637"><span class="linenos">637</span></a>        <span class="n">ack_wait_sec</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">int</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">15</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-638"><a href="#Memphis-638"><span class="linenos">638</span></a>        <span class="n">headers</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">Union</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">Headers</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="kc">None</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="kc">None</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-639"><a href="#Memphis-639"><span class="linenos">639</span></a>        <span class="n">async_produce</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">bool</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="kc">False</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-640"><a href="#Memphis-640"><span class="linenos">640</span></a>        <span class="n">msg_id</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">Union</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="nb">str</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="kc">None</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="kc">None</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-641"><a href="#Memphis-641"><span class="linenos">641</span></a>    <span class="p">):</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-642"><a href="#Memphis-642"><span class="linenos">642</span></a><span class="w">        </span><span class="sd">&quot;&quot;&quot;Produces a message into a station without the need to create a producer.</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-643"><a href="#Memphis-643"><span class="linenos">643</span></a><span class="sd">        Args:</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-644"><a href="#Memphis-644"><span class="linenos">644</span></a><span class="sd">            station_name (str): station name to produce messages into.</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-645"><a href="#Memphis-645"><span class="linenos">645</span></a><span class="sd">            producer_name (str): name for the producer.</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-646"><a href="#Memphis-646"><span class="linenos">646</span></a><span class="sd">            message (bytearray/dict): message to send into the station - bytearray/protobuf class (schema validated station - protobuf) or bytearray/dict (schema validated station - json schema) or string/bytearray/graphql.language.ast.DocumentNode (schema validated station - graphql schema or  bytearray/dict (schema validated station - avro schema))</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-647"><a href="#Memphis-647"><span class="linenos">647</span></a><span class="sd">            generate_random_suffix (bool): false by default, if true concatenate a random suffix to producer&#39;s name</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-648"><a href="#Memphis-648"><span class="linenos">648</span></a><span class="sd">            ack_wait_sec (int, optional): max time in seconds to wait for an ack from memphis. Defaults to 15.</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-649"><a href="#Memphis-649"><span class="linenos">649</span></a><span class="sd">            headers (dict, optional): Message headers, defaults to {}.</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-650"><a href="#Memphis-650"><span class="linenos">650</span></a><span class="sd">            async_produce (boolean, optional): produce operation won&#39;t wait for broker acknowledgement</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-651"><a href="#Memphis-651"><span class="linenos">651</span></a><span class="sd">            msg_id (string, optional): Attach msg-id header to the message in order to achieve idempotence</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-652"><a href="#Memphis-652"><span class="linenos">652</span></a><span class="sd">        Raises:</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-653"><a href="#Memphis-653"><span class="linenos">653</span></a><span class="sd">            Exception: _description_</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-654"><a href="#Memphis-654"><span class="linenos">654</span></a><span class="sd">        &quot;&quot;&quot;</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-655"><a href="#Memphis-655"><span class="linenos">655</span></a>        <span class="k">try</span><span class="p">:</span>

</span><span id="Memphis-657"><a href="#Memphis-657"><span class="linenos">657</span></a>            <span class="n">map_key</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">internal_station_name</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="s2">&quot;_&quot;</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="n">producer_name</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">lower</span><span class="p">()</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-658"><a href="#Memphis-658"><span class="linenos">658</span></a>            <span class="n">producer</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="kc">None</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-659"><a href="#Memphis-659"><span class="linenos">659</span></a>            <span class="k">if</span> <span class="n">map_key</span> <span class="ow">in</span> <span class="bp">self</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">producers_map</span><span class="p">:</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-660"><a href="#Memphis-660"><span class="linenos">660</span></a>                <span class="n">producer</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="bp">self</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">producers_map</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">map_key</span><span class="p">]</span>

</span><span id="Memphis-663"><a href="#Memphis-663"><span class="linenos">663</span></a>                    <span class="n">station_name</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="n">station_name</span><span class="p">,</span>

</span><span id="Memphis-673"><a href="#Memphis-673"><span class="linenos">673</span></a>            <span class="p">)</span>

</span><span id="Memphis-676"><a href="#Memphis-676"><span class="linenos">676</span></a>
</span><span id="Memphis-677"><a href="#Memphis-677"><span class="linenos">677</span></a>    <span class="k">async</span> <span class="k">def</span> <span class="nf">fetch_messages</span><span class="p">(</span>

</span><span id="Memphis-680"><a href="#Memphis-680"><span class="linenos">680</span></a>        <span class="n">consumer_name</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">str</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-681"><a href="#Memphis-681"><span class="linenos">681</span></a>        <span class="n">consumer_group</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">str</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="s2">&quot;&quot;</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-682"><a href="#Memphis-682"><span class="linenos">682</span></a>        <span class="n">batch_size</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">int</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">10</span><span class="p">,</span>

</span><span id="Memphis-684"><a href="#Memphis-684"><span class="linenos">684</span></a>        <span class="n">max_ack_time_ms</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">int</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">30000</span><span class="p">,</span>

</span><span id="Memphis-686"><a href="#Memphis-686"><span class="linenos">686</span></a>        <span class="n">generate_random_suffix</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">bool</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="kc">False</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-687"><a href="#Memphis-687"><span class="linenos">687</span></a>        <span class="n">start_consume_from_sequence</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">int</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-688"><a href="#Memphis-688"><span class="linenos">688</span></a>        <span class="n">last_messages</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">int</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-689"><a href="#Memphis-689"><span class="linenos">689</span></a>    <span class="p">):</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-690"><a href="#Memphis-690"><span class="linenos">690</span></a><span class="w">        </span><span class="sd">&quot;&quot;&quot;Consume a batch of messages.</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-691"><a href="#Memphis-691"><span class="linenos">691</span></a><span class="sd">        Args:.</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-692"><a href="#Memphis-692"><span class="linenos">692</span></a><span class="sd">            station_name (str): station name to consume messages from.</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-693"><a href="#Memphis-693"><span class="linenos">693</span></a><span class="sd">            consumer_name (str): name for the consumer.</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-694"><a href="#Memphis-694"><span class="linenos">694</span></a><span class="sd">            consumer_group (str, optional): consumer group name. Defaults to the consumer name.</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-695"><a href="#Memphis-695"><span class="linenos">695</span></a><span class="sd">            batch_size (int, optional): pull batch size. Defaults to 10.</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-696"><a href="#Memphis-696"><span class="linenos">696</span></a><span class="sd">            batch_max_time_to_wait_ms (int, optional): max time in miliseconds to wait between pulls. Defaults to 5000.</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-697"><a href="#Memphis-697"><span class="linenos">697</span></a><span class="sd">            max_ack_time_ms (int, optional): max time for ack a message in miliseconds, in case a message not acked in this time period the Memphis broker will resend it. Defaults to 30000.</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-698"><a href="#Memphis-698"><span class="linenos">698</span></a><span class="sd">            max_msg_deliveries (int, optional): max number of message deliveries, by default is 10.</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-699"><a href="#Memphis-699"><span class="linenos">699</span></a><span class="sd">            generate_random_suffix (bool): false by default, if true concatenate a random suffix to consumer&#39;s name</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-700"><a href="#Memphis-700"><span class="linenos">700</span></a><span class="sd">            start_consume_from_sequence(int, optional): start consuming from a specific sequence. defaults to 1.</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-701"><a href="#Memphis-701"><span class="linenos">701</span></a><span class="sd">            last_messages: consume the last N messages, defaults to -1 (all messages in the station).</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-702"><a href="#Memphis-702"><span class="linenos">702</span></a><span class="sd">        Returns:</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-703"><a href="#Memphis-703"><span class="linenos">703</span></a><span class="sd">            list: Message</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-704"><a href="#Memphis-704"><span class="linenos">704</span></a><span class="sd">        &quot;&quot;&quot;</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-705"><a href="#Memphis-705"><span class="linenos">705</span></a>        <span class="k">try</span><span class="p">:</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-706"><a href="#Memphis-706"><span class="linenos">706</span></a>            <span class="n">consumer</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="kc">None</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-707"><a href="#Memphis-707"><span class="linenos">707</span></a>            <span class="k">if</span> <span class="ow">not</span> <span class="bp">self</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">is_connection_active</span><span class="p">:</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-708"><a href="#Memphis-708"><span class="linenos">708</span></a>                <span class="k">raise</span> <span class="n">MemphisError</span><span class="p">(</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-709"><a href="#Memphis-709"><span class="linenos">709</span></a>                    <span class="s2">&quot;Cant fetch messages without being connected!&quot;</span><span class="p">)</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-710"><a href="#Memphis-710"><span class="linenos">710</span></a>            <span class="k">if</span> <span class="n">batch_size</span> <span class="o">&gt;</span> <span class="bp">self</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">MAX_BATCH_SIZE</span><span class="p">:</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-711"><a href="#Memphis-711"><span class="linenos">711</span></a>                <span class="k">raise</span> <span class="n">MemphisError</span><span class="p">(</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-712"><a href="#Memphis-712"><span class="linenos">712</span></a>                    <span class="sa">f</span><span class="s2">&quot;Batch size can not be greater than </span><span class="si">{</span><span class="bp">self</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">MAX_BATCH_SIZE</span><span class="si">}</span><span class="s2">&quot;</span><span class="p">)</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-713"><a href="#Memphis-713"><span class="linenos">713</span></a>            <span class="n">internal_station_name</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">get_internal_name</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">station_name</span><span class="p">)</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-714"><a href="#Memphis-714"><span class="linenos">714</span></a>            <span class="n">consumer_map_key</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">internal_station_name</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="s2">&quot;_&quot;</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="n">consumer_name</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">lower</span><span class="p">()</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-715"><a href="#Memphis-715"><span class="linenos">715</span></a>            <span class="k">if</span> <span class="n">consumer_map_key</span> <span class="ow">in</span> <span class="bp">self</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">consumers_map</span><span class="p">:</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-716"><a href="#Memphis-716"><span class="linenos">716</span></a>                <span class="n">consumer</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="bp">self</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">consumers_map</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">consumer_map_key</span><span class="p">]</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-717"><a href="#Memphis-717"><span class="linenos">717</span></a>            <span class="k">else</span><span class="p">:</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-718"><a href="#Memphis-718"><span class="linenos">718</span></a>                <span class="n">consumer</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="k">await</span> <span class="bp">self</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">consumer</span><span class="p">(</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-719"><a href="#Memphis-719"><span class="linenos">719</span></a>                    <span class="n">station_name</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="n">station_name</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-720"><a href="#Memphis-720"><span class="linenos">720</span></a>                    <span class="n">consumer_name</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="n">consumer_name</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-721"><a href="#Memphis-721"><span class="linenos">721</span></a>                    <span class="n">consumer_group</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="n">consumer_group</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-722"><a href="#Memphis-722"><span class="linenos">722</span></a>                    <span class="n">batch_size</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="n">batch_size</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-723"><a href="#Memphis-723"><span class="linenos">723</span></a>                    <span class="n">batch_max_time_to_wait_ms</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="n">batch_max_time_to_wait_ms</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-724"><a href="#Memphis-724"><span class="linenos">724</span></a>                    <span class="n">max_ack_time_ms</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="n">max_ack_time_ms</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-725"><a href="#Memphis-725"><span class="linenos">725</span></a>                    <span class="n">max_msg_deliveries</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="n">max_msg_deliveries</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-726"><a href="#Memphis-726"><span class="linenos">726</span></a>                    <span class="n">generate_random_suffix</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="n">generate_random_suffix</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-727"><a href="#Memphis-727"><span class="linenos">727</span></a>                    <span class="n">start_consume_from_sequence</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="n">start_consume_from_sequence</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-728"><a href="#Memphis-728"><span class="linenos">728</span></a>                    <span class="n">last_messages</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="n">last_messages</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-729"><a href="#Memphis-729"><span class="linenos">729</span></a>                <span class="p">)</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-730"><a href="#Memphis-730"><span class="linenos">730</span></a>            <span class="n">messages</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="k">await</span> <span class="n">consumer</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">fetch</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">batch_size</span><span class="p">)</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-731"><a href="#Memphis-731"><span class="linenos">731</span></a>            <span class="k">if</span> <span class="n">messages</span> <span class="o">==</span> <span class="kc">None</span><span class="p">:</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-732"><a href="#Memphis-732"><span class="linenos">732</span></a>                <span class="n">messages</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="p">[]</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-733"><a href="#Memphis-733"><span class="linenos">733</span></a>            <span class="k">return</span> <span class="n">messages</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-734"><a href="#Memphis-734"><span class="linenos">734</span></a>        <span class="k">except</span> <span class="ne">Exception</span> <span class="k">as</span> <span class="n">e</span><span class="p">:</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-735"><a href="#Memphis-735"><span class="linenos">735</span></a>            <span class="k">raise</span> <span class="n">MemphisError</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="nb">str</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">e</span><span class="p">))</span> <span class="kn">from</span> <span class="nn">e</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-736"><a href="#Memphis-736"><span class="linenos">736</span></a>
</span><span id="Memphis-737"><a href="#Memphis-737"><span class="linenos">737</span></a>    <span class="k">async</span> <span class="k">def</span> <span class="nf">create_schema</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="bp">self</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">schema_name</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">schema_type</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">schema_path</span><span class="p">):</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-738"><a href="#Memphis-738"><span class="linenos">738</span></a>
</span><span id="Memphis-739"><a href="#Memphis-739"><span class="linenos">739</span></a><span class="w">        </span><span class="sd">&quot;&quot;&quot;Creates a new schema.</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-740"><a href="#Memphis-740"><span class="linenos">740</span></a><span class="sd">        Args:.</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-741"><a href="#Memphis-741"><span class="linenos">741</span></a><span class="sd">            schema_name (str): the name of the schema.</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-742"><a href="#Memphis-742"><span class="linenos">742</span></a><span class="sd">            schema_type (str): the type of the schema json / graphql / protobuf / avro.</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-743"><a href="#Memphis-743"><span class="linenos">743</span></a><span class="sd">            schema_path (str): the path for the schema file</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-744"><a href="#Memphis-744"><span class="linenos">744</span></a><span class="sd">        &quot;&quot;&quot;</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-745"><a href="#Memphis-745"><span class="linenos">745</span></a>
</span><span id="Memphis-746"><a href="#Memphis-746"><span class="linenos">746</span></a>        <span class="k">if</span> <span class="n">schema_type</span> <span class="ow">not</span> <span class="ow">in</span> <span class="p">{</span><span class="s1">&#39;json&#39;</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="s1">&#39;graphql&#39;</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="s1">&#39;protobuf&#39;</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="s1">&#39;avro&#39;</span><span class="p">}:</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-747"><a href="#Memphis-747"><span class="linenos">747</span></a>            <span class="k">raise</span> <span class="n">MemphisError</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s2">&quot;schema type not supported&quot;</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="nb">type</span><span class="p">)</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-748"><a href="#Memphis-748"><span class="linenos">748</span></a>
</span><span id="Memphis-749"><a href="#Memphis-749"><span class="linenos">749</span></a>        <span class="k">try</span><span class="p">:</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-750"><a href="#Memphis-750"><span class="linenos">750</span></a>            <span class="k">await</span> <span class="bp">self</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">schema_name_validation</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">schema_name</span><span class="p">)</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-751"><a href="#Memphis-751"><span class="linenos">751</span></a>        <span class="k">except</span> <span class="ne">Exception</span> <span class="k">as</span> <span class="n">e</span><span class="p">:</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-752"><a href="#Memphis-752"><span class="linenos">752</span></a>            <span class="k">raise</span> <span class="n">e</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-753"><a href="#Memphis-753"><span class="linenos">753</span></a>
</span><span id="Memphis-754"><a href="#Memphis-754"><span class="linenos">754</span></a>
</span><span id="Memphis-755"><a href="#Memphis-755"><span class="linenos">755</span></a>        <span class="n">schema_content</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="s2">&quot;&quot;</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-756"><a href="#Memphis-756"><span class="linenos">756</span></a>        <span class="k">with</span> <span class="nb">open</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">schema_path</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="s2">&quot;rt&quot;</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">encoding</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="s2">&quot;utf-8&quot;</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="k">as</span> <span class="n">f</span><span class="p">:</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-757"><a href="#Memphis-757"><span class="linenos">757</span></a>            <span class="n">schema_content</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">f</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">read</span><span class="p">()</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-758"><a href="#Memphis-758"><span class="linenos">758</span></a>
</span><span id="Memphis-759"><a href="#Memphis-759"><span class="linenos">759</span></a>        <span class="n">create_schema_req</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="p">{</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-760"><a href="#Memphis-760"><span class="linenos">760</span></a>            <span class="s2">&quot;name&quot;</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">schema_name</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-761"><a href="#Memphis-761"><span class="linenos">761</span></a>            <span class="s2">&quot;type&quot;</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">schema_type</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-762"><a href="#Memphis-762"><span class="linenos">762</span></a>            <span class="s2">&quot;created_by_username&quot;</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="bp">self</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">username</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-763"><a href="#Memphis-763"><span class="linenos">763</span></a>            <span class="s2">&quot;schema_content&quot;</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">schema_content</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-764"><a href="#Memphis-764"><span class="linenos">764</span></a>            <span class="s2">&quot;message_struct_name&quot;</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="s2">&quot;&quot;</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-765"><a href="#Memphis-765"><span class="linenos">765</span></a>        <span class="p">}</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-766"><a href="#Memphis-766"><span class="linenos">766</span></a>
</span><span id="Memphis-767"><a href="#Memphis-767"><span class="linenos">767</span></a>        <span class="n">create_schema_req_bytes</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">json</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">dumps</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">create_schema_req</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">indent</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="mi">2</span><span class="p">)</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">encode</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s2">&quot;utf-8&quot;</span><span class="p">)</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-768"><a href="#Memphis-768"><span class="linenos">768</span></a>
</span><span id="Memphis-769"><a href="#Memphis-769"><span class="linenos">769</span></a>        <span class="n">create_res</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="k">await</span> <span class="bp">self</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">broker_manager</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">request</span><span class="p">(</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-770"><a href="#Memphis-770"><span class="linenos">770</span></a>            <span class="s2">&quot;$memphis_schema_creations&quot;</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">create_schema_req_bytes</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">timeout</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="mi">5</span><span class="p">)</span>

</span><span id="Memphis-772"><a href="#Memphis-772"><span class="linenos">772</span></a>        <span class="n">create_res</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">create_res</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">data</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">decode</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s2">&quot;utf-8&quot;</span><span class="p">)</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-773"><a href="#Memphis-773"><span class="linenos">773</span></a>        <span class="n">create_res</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">json</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">loads</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">create_res</span><span class="p">)</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-774"><a href="#Memphis-774"><span class="linenos">774</span></a>        <span class="k">if</span> <span class="n">create_res</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="s2">&quot;error&quot;</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="o">!=</span> <span class="s2">&quot;&quot;</span><span class="p">:</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-775"><a href="#Memphis-775"><span class="linenos">775</span></a>            <span class="k">raise</span> <span class="n">MemphisError</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">create_res</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="s2">&quot;error&quot;</span><span class="p">])</span>
