</span><span id="Memphis-778"><a href="#Memphis-778"><span class="linenos">778</span></a>    <span class="k">async</span> <span class="k">def</span> <span class="nf">schema_name_validation</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="bp">self</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">schema_name</span><span class="p">):</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-779"><a href="#Memphis-779"><span class="linenos">779</span></a>        <span class="k">if</span> <span class="nb">len</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">schema_name</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="o">==</span> <span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">:</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-780"><a href="#Memphis-780"><span class="linenos">780</span></a>            <span class="k">raise</span> <span class="n">MemphisError</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s2">&quot;Schema name cannot be empty&quot;</span><span class="p">)</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-781"><a href="#Memphis-781"><span class="linenos">781</span></a>
</span><span id="Memphis-782"><a href="#Memphis-782"><span class="linenos">782</span></a>        <span class="k">if</span> <span class="nb">len</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">schema_name</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="o">&gt;</span> <span class="mi">128</span><span class="p">:</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-783"><a href="#Memphis-783"><span class="linenos">783</span></a>            <span class="k">raise</span> <span class="n">MemphisError</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s2">&quot;Schema name should be under 128 characters&quot;</span><span class="p">)</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-784"><a href="#Memphis-784"><span class="linenos">784</span></a>
</span><span id="Memphis-785"><a href="#Memphis-785"><span class="linenos">785</span></a>        <span class="k">if</span> <span class="n">re</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">fullmatch</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="sa">r</span><span class="s1">&#39;^[a-z0-9_.-]*$&#39;</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">schema_name</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="ow">is</span> <span class="kc">None</span><span class="p">:</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-786"><a href="#Memphis-786"><span class="linenos">786</span></a>            <span class="k">raise</span> <span class="n">MemphisError</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s2">&quot;Only alphanumeric and the &#39;_&#39;, &#39;-&#39;, &#39;.&#39; characters are allowed in the schema name&quot;</span><span class="p">)</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-787"><a href="#Memphis-787"><span class="linenos">787</span></a>
</span><span id="Memphis-788"><a href="#Memphis-788"><span class="linenos">788</span></a>        <span class="k">if</span> <span class="ow">not</span> <span class="n">schema_name</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">]</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">isalnum</span><span class="p">()</span> <span class="ow">or</span> <span class="ow">not</span> <span class="n">schema_name</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">]</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">isalnum</span><span class="p">():</span>
</span><span id="Memphis-789"><a href="#Memphis-789"><span class="linenos">789</span></a>            <span class="k">raise</span> <span class="n">MemphisError</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s2">&quot;Schema name cannot start or end with a non-alphanumeric character&quot;</span><span class="p">)</span>

</span><span id="Memphis.connect-214"><a href="#Memphis.connect-214"><span class="linenos">214</span></a>        <span class="k">except</span> <span class="ne">Exception</span> <span class="k">as</span> <span class="n">e</span><span class="p">:</span>
</span><span id="Memphis.connect-215"><a href="#Memphis.connect-215"><span class="linenos">215</span></a>            <span class="k">raise</span> <span class="n">MemphisError</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="nb">str</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">e</span><span class="p">))</span>
</span></pre></div>


<div class="docstring"><p>Creates connection with Memphis.
Args:
host (str): memphis host.
username (str): user of type root/application.
account_id (int): You can find it on the profile page in the Memphis UI. This field should be sent only on the cloud version of Memphis, otherwise it will be ignored
connection_token (str): connection token.
password (str): depends on how Memphis deployed - default is connection token-based authentication.
port (int, optional): port. Defaults to 6666.
reconnect (bool, optional): whether to do reconnect while connection is lost. Defaults to True.
max_reconnect (int, optional): The reconnect attempt. Defaults to 3.
reconnect_interval_ms (int, optional): Interval in milliseconds between reconnect attempts. Defaults to 200.
timeout_ms (int, optional): connection timeout in milliseconds. Defaults to 15000.
key_file (string): path to tls key file.
cert_file (string): path to tls cert file.
ca_file (string): path to tls ca file.</p>
</div>


</div>

</span><span id="Memphis.station-233"><a href="#Memphis.station-233"><span class="linenos">233</span></a>        <span class="n">tiered_storage_enabled</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">bool</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="kc">False</span><span class="p">,</span>

</span><span id="Memphis.station-279"><a href="#Memphis.station-279"><span class="linenos">279</span></a>            <span class="k">if</span> <span class="nb">str</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">e</span><span class="p">)</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">find</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s2">&quot;already exist&quot;</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="o">!=</span> <span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">:</span>
</span><span id="Memphis.station-280"><a href="#Memphis.station-280"><span class="linenos">280</span></a>                <span class="k">return</span> <span class="n">Station</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="bp">self</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">name</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">lower</span><span class="p">())</span>
</span><span id="Memphis.station-281"><a href="#Memphis.station-281"><span class="linenos">281</span></a>            <span class="k">raise</span> <span class="n">MemphisError</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="nb">str</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">e</span><span class="p">))</span> <span class="kn">from</span> <span class="nn">e</span>
</span></pre></div>


<div class="docstring"><p>Creates a station.
Args:
name (str): station name.
retention_type (Retention, optional): retention type: MESSAGE_AGE_SEC/MESSAGES/BYTES/ACK_BASED . Defaults to "MESSAGE_AGE_SEC".
retention_value (int, optional): number which represents the retention based on the retention_type. Defaults to 604800.
storage_type (Storage, optional): persistance storage for messages of the station: disk/memory. Defaults to "disk".
replicas (int, optional):number of replicas for the messages of the data. Defaults to 1.
idempotency_window_ms (int, optional): time frame in which idempotent messages will be tracked, happens based on message ID Defaults to 120000.
schema_name (str): schema name.
Returns:
object: station</p>
</div>


</div>

<div class="docstring"><p>Creates a producer.
Args:
station_name (str): station name to produce messages into.
producer_name (str): name for the producer.
generate_random_suffix (bool): false by default, if true concatenate a random suffix to producer's name
Raises:
Exception: _description_
Returns:
_type_: _description_</p>
</div>

</span><span id="Memphis.consumer-543"><a href="#Memphis.consumer-543"><span class="linenos">543</span></a>        <span class="n">generate_random_suffix</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">bool</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="kc">False</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="Memphis.consumer-544"><a href="#Memphis.consumer-544"><span class="linenos">544</span></a>        <span class="n">start_consume_from_sequence</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">int</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span>

</span><span id="Memphis.consumer-547"><a href="#Memphis.consumer-547"><span class="linenos">547</span></a><span class="w">        </span><span class="sd">&quot;&quot;&quot;Creates a consumer.</span>
</span><span id="Memphis.consumer-548"><a href="#Memphis.consumer-548"><span class="linenos">548</span></a><span class="sd">        Args:.</span>
</span><span id="Memphis.consumer-549"><a href="#Memphis.consumer-549"><span class="linenos">549</span></a><span class="sd">            station_name (str): station name to consume messages from.</span>
</span><span id="Memphis.consumer-550"><a href="#Memphis.consumer-550"><span class="linenos">550</span></a><span class="sd">            consumer_name (str): name for the consumer.</span>
</span><span id="Memphis.consumer-551"><a href="#Memphis.consumer-551"><span class="linenos">551</span></a><span class="sd">            consumer_group (str, optional): consumer group name. Defaults to the consumer name.</span>
</span><span id="Memphis.consumer-552"><a href="#Memphis.consumer-552"><span class="linenos">552</span></a><span class="sd">            pull_interval_ms (int, optional): interval in milliseconds between pulls. Defaults to 1000.</span>
</span><span id="Memphis.consumer-553"><a href="#Memphis.consumer-553"><span class="linenos">553</span></a><span class="sd">            batch_size (int, optional): pull batch size. Defaults to 10.</span>
</span><span id="Memphis.consumer-554"><a href="#Memphis.consumer-554"><span class="linenos">554</span></a><span class="sd">            batch_max_time_to_wait_ms (int, optional): max time in milliseconds to wait between pulls. Defaults to 5000.</span>
</span><span id="Memphis.consumer-555"><a href="#Memphis.consumer-555"><span class="linenos">555</span></a><span class="sd">            max_ack_time_ms (int, optional): max time for ack a message in milliseconds, in case a message not acked in this time period the Memphis broker will resend it. Defaults to 30000.</span>
</span><span id="Memphis.consumer-556"><a href="#Memphis.consumer-556"><span class="linenos">556</span></a><span class="sd">            max_msg_deliveries (int, optional): max number of message deliveries, by default is 10.</span>
</span><span id="Memphis.consumer-557"><a href="#Memphis.consumer-557"><span class="linenos">557</span></a><span class="sd">            generate_random_suffix (bool): false by default, if true concatenate a random suffix to consumer&#39;s name</span>
</span><span id="Memphis.consumer-558"><a href="#Memphis.consumer-558"><span class="linenos">558</span></a><span class="sd">            start_consume_from_sequence(int, optional): start consuming from a specific sequence. defaults to 1.</span>
</span><span id="Memphis.consumer-559"><a href="#Memphis.consumer-559"><span class="linenos">559</span></a><span class="sd">            last_messages: consume the last N messages, defaults to -1 (all messages in the station).</span>
</span><span id="Memphis.consumer-560"><a href="#Memphis.consumer-560"><span class="linenos">560</span></a><span class="sd">        Returns:</span>
</span><span id="Memphis.consumer-561"><a href="#Memphis.consumer-561"><span class="linenos">561</span></a><span class="sd">            object: consumer</span>
</span><span id="Memphis.consumer-562"><a href="#Memphis.consumer-562"><span class="linenos">562</span></a><span class="sd">        &quot;&quot;&quot;</span>
</span><span id="Memphis.consumer-563"><a href="#Memphis.consumer-563"><span class="linenos">563</span></a>        <span class="k">try</span><span class="p">:</span>

</span><span id="Memphis.consumer-566"><a href="#Memphis.consumer-566"><span class="linenos">566</span></a>            <span class="k">if</span> <span class="n">batch_size</span> <span class="o">&gt;</span> <span class="bp">self</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">MAX_BATCH_SIZE</span><span class="p">:</span>

</span><span id="Memphis.consumer-569"><a href="#Memphis.consumer-569"><span class="linenos">569</span></a>            <span class="n">real_name</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">consumer_name</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">lower</span><span class="p">()</span>

</span><span id="Memphis.consumer-577"><a href="#Memphis.consumer-577"><span class="linenos">577</span></a>                <span class="p">)</span>
</span><span id="Memphis.consumer-578"><a href="#Memphis.consumer-578"><span class="linenos">578</span></a>
</span><span id="Memphis.consumer-579"><a href="#Memphis.consumer-579"><span class="linenos">579</span></a>            <span class="k">if</span> <span class="n">last_messages</span> <span class="o">&lt;</span> <span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">:</span>

</span><span id="Memphis.consumer-611"><a href="#Memphis.consumer-611"><span class="linenos">611</span></a>            <span class="n">internal_station_name</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">get_internal_name</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">station_name</span><span class="p">)</span>
</span><span id="Memphis.consumer-612"><a href="#Memphis.consumer-612"><span class="linenos">612</span></a>            <span class="n">map_key</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">internal_station_name</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="s2">&quot;_&quot;</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="n">real_name</span>
</span><span id="Memphis.consumer-613"><a href="#Memphis.consumer-613"><span class="linenos">613</span></a>            <span class="n">consumer</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">Consumer</span><span class="p">(</span>
</span><span id="Memphis.consumer-614"><a href="#Memphis.consumer-614"><span class="linenos">614</span></a>                <span class="bp">self</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="Memphis.consumer-615"><a href="#Memphis.consumer-615"><span class="linenos">615</span></a>                <span class="n">station_name</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="Memphis.consumer-616"><a href="#Memphis.consumer-616"><span class="linenos">616</span></a>                <span class="n">consumer_name</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="Memphis.consumer-617"><a href="#Memphis.consumer-617"><span class="linenos">617</span></a>                <span class="n">cg</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="Memphis.consumer-618"><a href="#Memphis.consumer-618"><span class="linenos">618</span></a>                <span class="n">pull_interval_ms</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="Memphis.consumer-619"><a href="#Memphis.consumer-619"><span class="linenos">619</span></a>                <span class="n">batch_size</span><span class="p">,</span>

</span><span id="Memphis.consumer-621"><a href="#Memphis.consumer-621"><span class="linenos">621</span></a>                <span class="n">max_ack_time_ms</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="Memphis.consumer-622"><a href="#Memphis.consumer-622"><span class="linenos">622</span></a>                <span class="n">max_msg_deliveries</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="Memphis.consumer-623"><a href="#Memphis.consumer-623"><span class="linenos">623</span></a>                <span class="n">start_consume_from_sequence</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="n">start_consume_from_sequence</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="Memphis.consumer-624"><a href="#Memphis.consumer-624"><span class="linenos">624</span></a>                <span class="n">last_messages</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="n">last_messages</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="Memphis.consumer-625"><a href="#Memphis.consumer-625"><span class="linenos">625</span></a>            <span class="p">)</span>
</span><span id="Memphis.consumer-626"><a href="#Memphis.consumer-626"><span class="linenos">626</span></a>            <span class="bp">self</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">consumers_map</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">map_key</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">consumer</span>
</span><span id="Memphis.consumer-627"><a href="#Memphis.consumer-627"><span class="linenos">627</span></a>            <span class="k">return</span> <span class="n">consumer</span>
</span><span id="Memphis.consumer-628"><a href="#Memphis.consumer-628"><span class="linenos">628</span></a>        <span class="k">except</span> <span class="ne">Exception</span> <span class="k">as</span> <span class="n">e</span><span class="p">:</span>
</span><span id="Memphis.consumer-629"><a href="#Memphis.consumer-629"><span class="linenos">629</span></a>            <span class="k">raise</span> <span class="n">MemphisError</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="nb">str</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">e</span><span class="p">))</span> <span class="kn">from</span> <span class="nn">e</span>
</span></pre></div>


<div class="docstring"><p>Creates a consumer.
Args:.
station_name (str): station name to consume messages from.
consumer_name (str): name for the consumer.
consumer_group (str, optional): consumer group name. Defaults to the consumer name.
pull_interval_ms (int, optional): interval in milliseconds between pulls. Defaults to 1000.
batch_size (int, optional): pull batch size. Defaults to 10.
batch_max_time_to_wait_ms (int, optional): max time in milliseconds to wait between pulls. Defaults to 5000.
max_ack_time_ms (int, optional): max time for ack a message in milliseconds, in case a message not acked in this time period the Memphis broker will resend it. Defaults to 30000.
max_msg_deliveries (int, optional): max number of message deliveries, by default is 10.
generate_random_suffix (bool): false by default, if true concatenate a random suffix to consumer's name
start_consume_from_sequence(int, optional): start consuming from a specific sequence. defaults to 1.
last_messages: consume the last N messages, defaults to -1 (all messages in the station).
Returns:
object: consumer</p>
</div>


</div>

</span><span id="Memphis.produce-637"><a href="#Memphis.produce-637"><span class="linenos">637</span></a>        <span class="n">ack_wait_sec</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">int</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">15</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="Memphis.produce-638"><a href="#Memphis.produce-638"><span class="linenos">638</span></a>        <span class="n">headers</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">Union</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">Headers</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="kc">None</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="kc">None</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="Memphis.produce-639"><a href="#Memphis.produce-639"><span class="linenos">639</span></a>        <span class="n">async_produce</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">bool</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="kc">False</span><span class="p">,</span>

</span><span id="Memphis.produce-641"><a href="#Memphis.produce-641"><span class="linenos">641</span></a>    <span class="p">):</span>
</span><span id="Memphis.produce-642"><a href="#Memphis.produce-642"><span class="linenos">642</span></a><span class="w">        </span><span class="sd">&quot;&quot;&quot;Produces a message into a station without the need to create a producer.</span>
</span><span id="Memphis.produce-643"><a href="#Memphis.produce-643"><span class="linenos">643</span></a><span class="sd">        Args:</span>
</span><span id="Memphis.produce-644"><a href="#Memphis.produce-644"><span class="linenos">644</span></a><span class="sd">            station_name (str): station name to produce messages into.</span>
</span><span id="Memphis.produce-645"><a href="#Memphis.produce-645"><span class="linenos">645</span></a><span class="sd">            producer_name (str): name for the producer.</span>
</span><span id="Memphis.produce-646"><a href="#Memphis.produce-646"><span class="linenos">646</span></a><span class="sd">            message (bytearray/dict): message to send into the station - bytearray/protobuf class (schema validated station - protobuf) or bytearray/dict (schema validated station - json schema) or string/bytearray/graphql.language.ast.DocumentNode (schema validated station - graphql schema or  bytearray/dict (schema validated station - avro schema))</span>
</span><span id="Memphis.produce-647"><a href="#Memphis.produce-647"><span class="linenos">647</span></a><span class="sd">            generate_random_suffix (bool): false by default, if true concatenate a random suffix to producer&#39;s name</span>
</span><span id="Memphis.produce-648"><a href="#Memphis.produce-648"><span class="linenos">648</span></a><span class="sd">            ack_wait_sec (int, optional): max time in seconds to wait for an ack from memphis. Defaults to 15.</span>
</span><span id="Memphis.produce-649"><a href="#Memphis.produce-649"><span class="linenos">649</span></a><span class="sd">            headers (dict, optional): Message headers, defaults to {}.</span>
</span><span id="Memphis.produce-650"><a href="#Memphis.produce-650"><span class="linenos">650</span></a><span class="sd">            async_produce (boolean, optional): produce operation won&#39;t wait for broker acknowledgement</span>
</span><span id="Memphis.produce-651"><a href="#Memphis.produce-651"><span class="linenos">651</span></a><span class="sd">            msg_id (string, optional): Attach msg-id header to the message in order to achieve idempotence</span>
</span><span id="Memphis.produce-652"><a href="#Memphis.produce-652"><span class="linenos">652</span></a><span class="sd">        Raises:</span>
</span><span id="Memphis.produce-653"><a href="#Memphis.produce-653"><span class="linenos">653</span></a><span class="sd">            Exception: _description_</span>
</span><span id="Memphis.produce-654"><a href="#Memphis.produce-654"><span class="linenos">654</span></a><span class="sd">        &quot;&quot;&quot;</span>
</span><span id="Memphis.produce-655"><a href="#Memphis.produce-655"><span class="linenos">655</span></a>        <span class="k">try</span><span class="p">:</span>
</span><span id="Memphis.produce-656"><a href="#Memphis.produce-656"><span class="linenos">656</span></a>            <span class="n">internal_station_name</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">get_internal_name</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">station_name</span><span class="p">)</span>

</span><span id="Memphis.produce-663"><a href="#Memphis.produce-663"><span class="linenos">663</span></a>                    <span class="n">station_name</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="n">station_name</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="Memphis.produce-664"><a href="#Memphis.produce-664"><span class="linenos">664</span></a>                    <span class="n">producer_name</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="n">producer_name</span><span class="p">,</span>

</span><span id="Memphis.produce-671"><a href="#Memphis.produce-671"><span class="linenos">671</span></a>                <span class="n">async_produce</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="n">async_produce</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="Memphis.produce-672"><a href="#Memphis.produce-672"><span class="linenos">672</span></a>                <span class="n">msg_id</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="n">msg_id</span><span class="p">,</span>
</span><span id="Memphis.produce-673"><a href="#Memphis.produce-673"><span class="linenos">673</span></a>            <span class="p">)</span>
</span><span id="Memphis.produce-674"><a href="#Memphis.produce-674"><span class="linenos">674</span></a>        <span class="k">except</span> <span class="ne">Exception</span> <span class="k">as</span> <span class="n">e</span><span class="p">:</span>
</span><span id="Memphis.produce-675"><a href="#Memphis.produce-675"><span class="linenos">675</span></a>            <span class="k">raise</span> <span class="n">MemphisError</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="nb">str</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">e</span><span class="p">))</span> <span class="kn">from</span> <span class="nn">e</span>
</span></pre></div>


<div class="docstring"><p>Produces a message into a station without the need to create a producer.
Args:
station_name (str): station name to produce messages into.
producer_name (str): name for the producer.
message (bytearray/dict): message to send into the station - bytearray/protobuf class (schema validated station - protobuf) or bytearray/dict (schema validated station - json schema) or string/bytearray/graphql.language.ast.DocumentNode (schema validated station - graphql schema or  bytearray/dict (schema validated station - avro schema))
generate_random_suffix (bool): false by default, if true concatenate a random suffix to producer's name
ack_wait_sec (int, optional): max time in seconds to wait for an ack from memphis. Defaults to 15.
headers (dict, optional): Message headers, defaults to {}.
async_produce (boolean, optional): produce operation won't wait for broker acknowledgement
msg_id (string, optional): Attach msg-id header to the message in order to achieve idempotence
Raises:
Exception: _description_</p>
</div>


</div>

</span><span id="Memphis.fetch_messages-731"><a href="#Memphis.fetch_messages-731"><span class="linenos">731</span></a>            <span class="k">if</span> <span class="n">messages</span> <span class="o">==</span> <span class="kc">None</span><span class="p">:</span>
</span><span id="Memphis.fetch_messages-732"><a href="#Memphis.fetch_messages-732"><span class="linenos">732</span></a>                <span class="n">messages</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="p">[]</span>
</span><span id="Memphis.fetch_messages-733"><a href="#Memphis.fetch_messages-733"><span class="linenos">733</span></a>            <span class="k">return</span> <span class="n">messages</span>
</span><span id="Memphis.fetch_messages-734"><a href="#Memphis.fetch_messages-734"><span class="linenos">734</span></a>        <span class="k">except</span> <span class="ne">Exception</span> <span class="k">as</span> <span class="n">e</span><span class="p">:</span>
</span><span id="Memphis.fetch_messages-735"><a href="#Memphis.fetch_messages-735"><span class="linenos">735</span></a>            <span class="k">raise</span> <span class="n">MemphisError</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="nb">str</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">e</span><span class="p">))</span> <span class="kn">from</span> <span class="nn">e</span>
</span></pre></div>


<div class="docstring"><p>Consume a batch of messages.
Args:.
station_name (str): station name to consume messages from.
consumer_name (str): name for the consumer.
consumer_group (str, optional): consumer group name. Defaults to the consumer name.
batch_size (int, optional): pull batch size. Defaults to 10.
batch_max_time_to_wait_ms (int, optional): max time in miliseconds to wait between pulls. Defaults to 5000.
max_ack_time_ms (int, optional): max time for ack a message in miliseconds, in case a message not acked in this time period the Memphis broker will resend it. Defaults to 30000.
max_msg_deliveries (int, optional): max number of message deliveries, by default is 10.
generate_random_suffix (bool): false by default, if true concatenate a random suffix to consumer's name
start_consume_from_sequence(int, optional): start consuming from a specific sequence. defaults to 1.
last_messages: consume the last N messages, defaults to -1 (all messages in the station).
Returns:
list: Message</p>
</div>


</div>
